behavior find_food_food_2074_around_kitchen_counter_122(food_food:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_food)
    body:
        assert is_food_food(food_food)
        bind kitchen_counter_instance:item where:
            is_kitchen_counter(kitchen_counter_instance) and id[kitchen_counter_instance]==122
        achieve close_char(char,kitchen_counter_instance)
        if can_open(kitchen_counter_instance):
            achieve_once open(kitchen_counter_instance)
            exp(food_food,kitchen_counter_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_food,kitchen_counter_instance)
    eff:

        close[food_food,kitchen_counter_instance]=True
        close[kitchen_counter_instance,food_food]=True

#goal_representation
 
behavior wash_vegetables(vegetable: item, sink: item):
    body:
        achieve inside(vegetable, sink)
        # Place each vegetable inside the sink

        if exists faucet: item: is_faucet(faucet) and close(faucet, sink):
            # Check if there is a faucet close to the sink
            bind faucet: item where:
                is_faucet(faucet) and close(faucet, sink)
            achieve_once is_on(faucet)
            # Turn on the faucet to wash vegetables

        wash(vegetable)
        # Wash the vegetable in the sink

        if exists faucet: item: is_faucet(faucet) and close(faucet, sink):
            bind faucet: item where:
                is_faucet(faucet) and close(faucet, sink)
            achieve_once is_off(faucet)
            # Turn off the faucet after washing

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink)
        # Select a sink for washing

        foreach vegetable: item:
            if is_food_vegetable(vegetable):
                wash_vegetables(vegetable, sink)
        # Wash all vegetables

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
def is_vegetable(item: item):
    # Determine if an item is a vegetable
    return is_food_vegetable(item)

behavior wash_vegetable(vegetable: item):
    body:
        wash(vegetable)
        # Wash the specific vegetable

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        foreach vegetable: item:
            if is_vegetable(vegetable) and dirty(vegetable):
                wash_vegetable(vegetable)
        # Wash all vegetables that are dirty

#goal_representation_end

behavior wash_vegetables(vegetable:item):
    body:
        wash(vegetable)
        # Wash the vegetable by hand

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        foreach vegetable: item:
            if is_food_vegetable(vegetable) and dirty(vegetable):
                wash_vegetables(vegetable)
        # Loop through all vegetables, washing each one that is dirty

behavior wash_all_vegetables(vegetable:item):
    body:
        wash(vegetable)
        # Wash the vegetable

        foreach vegetable: item:

        # For each dirty vegetable, wash it

def is_food_vegetable_and_dirty(vegetable: item):
    # Function to check if an item is a vegetable and dirty
    return is_food_vegetable(vegetable) and dirty(vegetable)

behavior wash_vegetables(vegetable: item):
    body:
        wash(vegetable)
        # Wash each vegetable

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        foreach vegetable: item:
            if is_food_vegetable_and_dirty(vegetable):
                wash_vegetables(vegetable)
        # Wash all identified dirty vegetables that are food vegetables

behavior find_food_food_2094_around_fridge_126(food_food:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_food)
    body:
        assert is_food_food(food_food)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==126
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_food,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_food,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_food]=False
        close[food_food,fridge_instance]=True
        close[fridge_instance,food_food]=True

behavior find_food_fruit_2095_around_cutting_board_2123(food_fruit:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_fruit)
    body:
        assert is_food_fruit(food_fruit)
        bind cutting_board_instance:item where:
            is_cutting_board(cutting_board_instance) and id[cutting_board_instance]==2123
        achieve close_char(char,cutting_board_instance)
        if can_open(cutting_board_instance):
            achieve_once open(cutting_board_instance)
            exp(food_fruit,cutting_board_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_fruit,cutting_board_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_fruit]=False
        close[food_fruit,cutting_board_instance]=True
        close[cutting_board_instance,food_fruit]=True

#goal_representation
 
def is_vegetable(obj: item):
    # Function to check if an item is a vegetable
    return is_food_vegetable(obj)

behavior wash_vegetable(vegetable:item):
    body:
        wash(vegetable)
        # Wash the vegetable thoroughly

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        foreach vegetable: item:
            if is_vegetable(vegetable) and dirty(vegetable):
                wash_vegetable(vegetable)
        # Wash all dirty vegetables

#goal_representation_end

behavior locate_and_wash_vegetables(vegetable:item):
    body:
        achieve clean(vegetable)
        # Ensure the vegetable is cleaned

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        foreach vegetable: item:
            if is_food_vegetable(vegetable) and dirty(vegetable):
                locate_and_wash_vegetables(vegetable)
        # Iterate over each vegetable and clean it if its dirty

#goal_representation
 
def is_dirty_vegetable(vegetable: item):
    # Function to check if a vegetable is dirty
    return is_food_vegetable(vegetable) and dirty(vegetable)

behavior wash_vegetable(vegetable:item, sink:item):
    body:
        achieve inside(vegetable, sink)
        # Ensure the vegetable is inside the sink

        if exists faucet:item: is_faucet(faucet) and close(faucet, sink):
            achieve_once is_on(faucet)
            wash(vegetable)
            achieve_once is_off(faucet)
        else:
            wash(vegetable)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink)
        # Select a sink

        foreach vegetable: item:
            if is_dirty_vegetable(vegetable):
                wash_vegetable(vegetable, sink)
        # For each dirty vegetable, wash it in the sink

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
def is_dirty_vegetable(vegetable: item):
    # Function to check if a vegetable is dirty
    return is_food_vegetable(vegetable) and dirty(vegetable)

behavior wash_vegetable(vegetable: item, sink: item, faucet: item):
    body:
        achieve inside(vegetable, sink)
        # Ensure the vegetable is inside the sink

        if close(faucet, sink):
            achieve_once is_on(faucet)
            wash(vegetable)
            achieve_once is_off(faucet)
        else:
            wash(vegetable)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink)
        # Select a sink

        bind faucet: item where:
            is_faucet(faucet) and close(faucet, sink)
        # Select a faucet close to the sink

        foreach vegetable: item:
            if is_dirty_vegetable(vegetable):
                wash_vegetable(vegetable, sink, faucet)
        # For each dirty vegetable, wash it in the sink

#goal_representation_end

def is_dirty_vegetable(vegetable: item):
    # Function to check if a vegetable is dirty
    return is_food_vegetable(vegetable) and dirty(vegetable)

behavior wash_vegetable(vegetable: item):

        # Wash each dirty vegetable

#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_food_2073_around_stove_2135(food_food:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_food)
    body:
        assert is_food_food(food_food)
        bind stove_instance:item where:
            is_stove(stove_instance) and id[stove_instance]==2135
        achieve close_char(char,stove_instance)
        if can_open(stove_instance):
            achieve_once open(stove_instance)
            exp(food_food,stove_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_food,stove_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_food]=False
        close[food_food,stove_instance]=True
        close[stove_instance,food_food]=True

behavior boil_vegetables_in_pot(pot:item, stove:item):
    body:
        achieve on(pot, stove) 
        # Place the pot on the stove
        achieve is_on(stove) 
        # Turn on the stove to boil the vegetables

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind pot: item where:
            is_pot(pot)
        # Identify the pot to use for boiling vegetables

        bind stove: item where:
            is_stove(stove)
        # Identify the stove where the pot will be placed

        bind vegetables: item where:
            is_food_vegetable(vegetables) and clean(vegetables)
        # Identify the cleaned vegetables

        achieve inside(vegetables, pot) 
        # Place the vegetables inside the pot

        boil_vegetables_in_pot(pot, stove) 
        # Initiate the boiling process on the stove

#goal_representation_end

behavior find_food_onion_2104_around_fryingpan_2154(food_onion:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_onion)
    body:
        assert is_food_onion(food_onion)
        bind fryingpan_instance:item where:
            is_fryingpan(fryingpan_instance) and id[fryingpan_instance]==2154
        achieve close_char(char,fryingpan_instance)
        if can_open(fryingpan_instance):
            achieve_once open(fryingpan_instance)
            exp(food_onion,fryingpan_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_onion,fryingpan_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_onion]=False
        close[food_onion,fryingpan_instance]=True
        close[fryingpan_instance,food_onion]=True

#goal_representation
 
behavior cool_boiled_vegetables(vegetables: item, pot: item, bowl: item):
    body:
        achieve inside(vegetables, pot)
        # Ensure the boiled vegetables are in the pot

        achieve has_water(bowl)
        achieve inside(vegetables, bowl)
        # Transfer vegetables to a bowl with water to cool

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind vegetables: item where:
            is_food_vegetable(vegetables)
        # Bind vegetables identified

        bind pot: item where:
            is_pot(pot)
        # Bind pot used for boiling

        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl)
        # Bind a bowl for cooling

        cool_boiled_vegetables(vegetables, pot, bowl)

#goal_representation_end

behavior find_food_fruit_2095_around_bowl_2141(food_fruit:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_fruit)
    body:
        assert is_food_fruit(food_fruit)
        bind bowl_instance:item where:
            is_bowl(bowl_instance) and id[bowl_instance]==2141
        achieve close_char(char,bowl_instance)
        if can_open(bowl_instance):
            achieve_once open(bowl_instance)
            exp(food_fruit,bowl_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_fruit,bowl_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_fruit]=False
        close[food_fruit,bowl_instance]=True
        close[bowl_instance,food_fruit]=True

        # Place the boiled vegetables inside the bowl to cool
